Typically, some verification of employment or income is involved (via pay stubs and bank statements), although according to one source, some payday lenders do not verify income or run credit checks. Individual companies and franchises have their own underwriting criteria.\r\n\r\n$ Reasons for using payday advance loan - There are five groups that have higher odds of having used payday loans: those without a four-year college degree; home renters; African Americans; those earning below $40,000 annually; and those who are separated or divorced.\" Most borrowers use payday loans to cover ordinary living expenses over the course of months, not unexpected emergencies over the course of weeks.
